define('utils/ResponsiveEvents', ['mixins/Events', 'utils/responsive', 'utils/throttle', 'vanillajs'],
function (Events, Responsive, Throttle) {
'use strict';
var lastWidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth;
var lastSizes = Responsive.currentBreakpoints();
var events = ['breakpoint'];
Responsive.breakpoints.forEach(function(size) {
events.push('over-' + size, 'under-' + size);
});
var delegate = Events.create(events);
delegate.onOver = function(size, fn) {
delegate.on('over-' + size, fn);
};
delegate.onUnder = function(size, fn) {
delegate.on('under-' + size, fn);
};
delegate.offOver = function(size, fn) {
delegate.off('over-' + size, fn);
};
delegate.offUnder = function(size, fn) {
delegate.off('under-' + size, fn);
};
function getChangedSizes(a, b, reverse) {
var aDiff = a.filter(function(x) { return b.indexOf(x) < 0; });
var bDiff = b.filter(function(x) { return a.indexOf(x) < 0; });
return reverse ? aDiff.reverse().concat(bDiff.reverse()) : aDiff.concat(bDiff);
}
function checkBreakpoints() {
var width = document.body.clientWidth;
if (width == lastWidth) {
return;
}
var expanded = width > lastWidth;
var sizes = Responsive.currentBreakpoints();
var diff = getChangedSizes(lastSizes, sizes, expanded);
diff.forEach(function(size) {
var prefix = expanded ? 'over-' : 'under-';
delegate.emit(prefix + size);
});
if (diff.length) {
delegate.emit('breakpoint', sizes[0]);
}
lastSizes = sizes;
lastWidth = width;
}
window.addEventListener('resize', Throttle(checkBreakpoints, 100));
return delegate;
});
define('overlays/styles/tooltip', ['vanillajs', 'api-mod', 'overlays/utils'], function(vanilla, api, util){
'use strict';
function buildDOM( dir, style, elementType ){
this.container = api.createElement( elementType||'span', {
'class': 'ui_overlay ui_tooltip arrow_' + util.getArrowDir(dir, this.sourceElement, this.domParent) + ' ' + style
});
this.arrow = api.createElement( 'div', {
'class': 'arrow'
});
this.container.appendChild( this.arrow );
this.inner = api.createElement( 'div', {
'class': 'body_text'
});
this.container.appendChild( this.inner );
this.contentElement = this.inner;
}
var Tooltip = function( elmt, dir, options, content, elementType ){
if (elmt) {
options = options || elmt.getAttribute( 'data-tooltip' );
elementType = elementType || elmt.getAttribute( 'data-elementtype' );
}
return function(){
buildDOM.call( this, dir, options, elementType );
this.updateContent( content );
};
};
return Tooltip;
});

}).on('hide', function(){

});
};
return option;
});

return function(slideDirection) {
return function() {
if (!slideDirection || slideDirections.indexOf(slideDirection) < 0) {
return;
}
var $container = $(this.container);
var duration = 250;
var oldShow = this.show.bind(this);
var oldHide = this.hide.bind(this);
var timer = null;
this.show = function() {
clearTimeout(timer);
$container.addClass('slide-in').addClass(slideDirection);
oldShow && oldShow();
setTimeout(function() { $container.addClass('slide'); }, 0);
};
this.hide = function() {
clearTimeout(timer);
$container.removeClass('slide');
timer = setTimeout(function() {
oldHide && oldHide();
}, duration);
};
};
};
});
define('overlays/position/fullside', [
'lib/jquery-amd',
'overlays/position/base',
'overlays/options/disableBodyScroll',
'common/Radio'
], function(
$, Position, disableBodyScroll, radio
){
'use strict';
function fullSide(isLeft) {
return function() {
var position = Position();
var stopScroll = disableBodyScroll(false);
function composed() {
position.call(this);
stopScroll.call(this);
}
composed.onPosition = position.onPosition = function(){
$(this.container).addClass('fullside').addClass(isLeft ? 'left' : 'right');
};
composed.offPosition = position.offPosition = function(){
$(this.container).removeClass('fullside').removeClass(isLeft ? 'left' : 'right');
};
radio('collapsible-layout').on("toggle", function(open) {
var container = $('.fullside');
if (open) {
_adjustForDeeplinkHeader(container);
}
else {
container.css("bottom", "0px");
}
});
return composed;
};
}
function _adjustForDeeplinkHeader(container) {
var containerHeight = container.height();
var offset = containerHeight - window.innerHeight;
if (offset > 0) {
container.css("bottom", offset + "px");
}
}
return {
left : fullSide(true),
right : fullSide(false)
};
});

function _init() {

function openSort(event, elmt) {
if (!this.sortOverlay) {
this.sortOverlay = new Overlay(placementElem,
fullside.right(),
new Modal(null, null, 'collapsed_content', null, null, sortFlyout),
windowShade('dark'),
slide('from_right'),
closeOnWindowshadeClick);
}
this.sortOverlay.show();
}
function clickSort(event, elmt) {
if (!elmt || elmt.className.match(RE_ACTIVE)) {
return false;
}
var newSortOrder = elmt.getAttribute("data-sortOrder");
if (!newSortOrder) { return; }
setTimeout(function(){
_setSortOrder(newSortOrder);
}, 0);
Tracking.trackEvent('attraction_sort_h', 'click', newSortOrder);
var tabOptions = Array.prototype.slice.call(sortFilterBar.querySelectorAll(".sort_option"));
var flyoutOptions =  Array.prototype.slice.call(sortFlyout.querySelectorAll(".sort_option"));
tabOptions.concat(flyoutOptions).forEach( function(option) {
var oldcls = option.className;
var newcls = oldcls.replace(RE_ACTIVE,"");
if (option.getAttribute("data-sortOrder")===newSortOrder) {
newcls += " active";
}
if (oldcls!==newcls) {
option.className = newcls;
}
});
var sortSummary = sortFilterBar.querySelector(".sort-summary");
var label = elmt.getAttribute("data-label");
sortSummary && label && (sortSummary.innerHTML=label);
this.sortOverlay && this.sortOverlay.hide();
}
function _setSortOrder(newSortOrder) {
var sortOrderKey = $('#sortOptions').data('sortOrderArgument');
var sortOrderArgument = '-a_' + sortOrderKey + '.';
var re;
var replacement = function(m, l) {
var value = newSortOrder || '';
return (value.length) ? sortOrderArgument + value : '';
}
var url = window.location.href;
if (/-j[^-]+/.test(url)) {
re = new RegExp(/(-j[^-]+)/g);
window.location = window.location.href.replace(re, replacement);
}
else if (/(\?|&)(j|sortOrder)=/.test(url)) {
re = new RegExp(/(\?|&)(j|sortOrder)=([^&]+)/g);
window.location = window.location.href.replace(re, "$1sortOrder=" + (newSortOrder || ''));
}
else if (/-a_(sort|sortOrder)/.test(url)) {
re = new RegExp(/-a_(sort|sortOrder)\.([^-]+)/g);
window.location = window.location.href.replace(re, replacement);
}
else if (/-g[\d]+/.test(url)) {
re = new RegExp(/(-g[\d]+)/g);
window.location = window.location.href.replace(re, "$&" + replacement());
}
else if (/-a_latitude/.test(url)) {
re = new RegExp(/(-a_latitude\.[^-]+)/g);
window.location = window.location.href.replace(re, "$&" + replacement());
}
}
function remove(evt, elt) {
var arg = elt.getAttribute('data-arg');
var replacement = '';
var re;
// Remove the value from multi-valued data-args that aren't delimited with '|'
var match = new RegExp('^(t|zfp|zfm)([^|]*)$').exec(arg);
if (match) {
var name = match[1];
var id = match[2];
re = new RegExp('-' + name + '([\\d,%2C]+)','g');
replacement = function(m, l) {
l = l.split(/,|%2C/)
.filter(function(v) { return v != id; });
return (l && l.length > 0) ? ('-' + name + l.join(',')) : '';
};
}
else {
re = new RegExp('('+
arg
.split('|')
.map(function(a){ return '-' + a; })
.join('|')
+ ')', 'g');
}
window.location = window.location.href.replace(re, replacement);
}
function openFilters(event, elmt) {
var cls = elmt.className;
if (cls.match(RE_LOADING)) {
return;
}
elmt.className = cls+" loading";
require(["trjs!responsive/collapsibleLayout"], function(c) {
elmt.className = cls;
c.toggle();
});
}
function inDestination(evt, elt) {
taEvent.fireEvent('event.placement.mobileAttractionCoverage.inDestination');
}
function _updateContent( contentElementSelector, content) {
var contentElement = placementElem.querySelector(contentElementSelector);
ajaxPreserves.setContentElement(contentElement, content, true);
contentElement = placementElem.querySelector(contentElementSelector);
prwidgets.initWidgets(contentElement);
}
function _updateOnRepoll(content) {
_updateContent('.ui_container', content);
this.init();
}
var _this = {
init: _init,
remove: remove,
openSort: openSort,
clickSort: clickSort,
openFilters: openFilters,
openNearMeTooltip: openNearMeTooltip,
inDestination: inDestination,
updateOnRepoll: _updateOnRepoll
};
_this.init();
taEvent.on('update-'+placement.id, function(content) { _this.updateOnRepoll(content); });
return _this;
});

/**

define(["placement"], function(placement) {
"use strict";
var container = window.z("#" + placement.id);
var misspellingsContainer = container.find(".reversion_module_container");
var reversionModuleFilterApplied = "reversionModuleFilterApplied";
var reversionModuleSRPResultClicked = "reversionModuleSRPResultClicked";
var originalQuery;
var searchSessionId;
z('body').on('parserCorrectResultSelected', storeResultListClick);
z('body').on('typeaheadEnterButtonPressed', clearReversionModuleLocalStorage);
z('body').on('reversionModuleFilterApplied', storeFilterSortInteraction);
function getSearchSessionId() {
var i;
var query = window.location.search.substring(1);
var params = query.split("&");
for (i = 0; i < params.length; i++) {
if (params[i].indexOf("searchSessionId") > -1) {
var searchParams = params[i].split("=");
return decodeURIComponent(searchParams[1]);
}
}
return "";
}
/**
* Checks if it is the hotels list page. If so, do not execute function (not compatible with hotel lite page, will
* result in JS errors on page load)
* Should be cleaned up with ticket NAV-4395
* @returns {boolean}
*/
function isHotelsListPage() {
return window.location.href.indexOf("hotel") > 0;
}
/**
* Initialize values for JS code
* @param query The original query
*/
function initialize(/* String */ query) {
if (isHotelsListPage())
{
return;
}
originalQuery = query;
searchSessionId = getSearchSessionId();
}
/**
* Reset local storage for reversion module when typeahead "enter" button clicked
*/
function clearReversionModuleLocalStorage() {
if (ta.util.localstorage.canUseLocalStore()) {
localStorage[reversionModuleSRPResultClicked] = JSON.stringify({value: false, query: ""});
localStorage[reversionModuleFilterApplied] = JSON.stringify({value: false, query: ""});
}
}
/**
* Store info on hiding reversion module if user interacts with filters
*/
function storeFilterSortInteraction() {
if(ta.util.localstorage.canUseLocalStore()) {
localStorage[reversionModuleFilterApplied] = JSON.stringify({value: true, query: originalQuery});
}
}
/**
* Store info on hiding reversion module if user choses a POI detail from results
*/
function storeResultListClick() {
if (ta.util.localstorage.canUseLocalStore()) {
localStorage[reversionModuleSRPResultClicked] = JSON.stringify({value: true, query: ""});
}
}
/**
* Record if user chooses the misspellings module to search for the original query verbatim
*/
function recordOriginalQueryClick() {
ta.setEvtCookie(searchSessionId, "parser_reversion_click", originalQuery, 0, "/MobileSearch");
}
/**
* Record if the reversion module was shown to user
*/
function recordOriginalQueryShow() {
if (isHotelsListPage())
{
return;
}
// If placement is supposed to be hidden, don't track misspellings placement as shown
if (ta.util.localstorage.canUseLocalStore()) {
if (localStorage[reversionModuleFilterApplied] !== undefined) {
var misspellingFilterAppliedObject = JSON.parse(localStorage[reversionModuleFilterApplied]);
if (misspellingFilterAppliedObject.value) {
return;
}
}
if(localStorage[reversionModuleSRPResultClicked] !== undefined) {
var misspellingsPoiClickedObject = JSON.parse(localStorage[reversionModuleSRPResultClicked]);
if (misspellingsPoiClickedObject.value) {
return;
}
}
}
ta.trackEventOnPage(searchSessionId, "parser_reversion_show", originalQuery, 0, true);
}
/**
* Record if user dismisses the reversion module
*/
function recordQueryDismiss() {
ta.trackEventOnPage(searchSessionId, "parser_reversion_dismiss", originalQuery, 0, true);
hideReversionModuleContainer();
}
/**
* Add class to hide reversion module
*/
function hideReversionModuleContainer() {
misspellingsContainer.addClass("hidden");
}
/**
* Check if reversion module should be hidden
*/
function checkIfHidePlacement() {
if (isHotelsListPage())
{
return;
}
if (ta.util.localstorage.canUseLocalStore()) {
// Checks to see if user selected a filter or sort for the corrected query from SRP
// If so, then do not display misspelling placement
if (localStorage[reversionModuleFilterApplied] !== undefined) {
var misspellingFilterAppliedObject = JSON.parse(localStorage[reversionModuleFilterApplied]);
if (misspellingFilterAppliedObject.value && misspellingFilterAppliedObject.query === originalQuery) {
hideReversionModuleContainer();
} else {
localStorage[reversionModuleFilterApplied] = JSON.stringify({value: false, query: ""});
}
}
// Check to see if user is returning from a POI page click to SRP with misspelling corrected
// If so, hide misspelling placement
if(localStorage[reversionModuleSRPResultClicked] !== undefined) {
var misspellingsPoiClickedObject = JSON.parse(localStorage[reversionModuleSRPResultClicked]);
if (misspellingsPoiClickedObject.value && misspellingsPoiClickedObject.query === originalQuery) {
hideReversionModuleContainer();
} else {
localStorage[reversionModuleSRPResultClicked] = JSON.stringify({value: false, query: ""});
}
}
}
}
return {
"initialize": initialize,
"recordOriginalQueryClick": recordOriginalQueryClick,
"recordOriginalQueryShow": recordOriginalQueryShow,
"hideReversionModuleContainer": hideReversionModuleContainer,
"checkIfHidePlacement": checkIfHidePlacement,
"recordQueryDismiss": recordQueryDismiss
};
});});require(['ta/prwidgets'], function(widgets) {

function _selectImage(index) {

$widget.find('.left_nav').addClass('hidden');

else {
$widget.find('.left_nav').removeClass('hidden');

$widget.find('.right_nav').addClass('hidden');
}
else {
$widget.find('.right_nav').removeClass('hidden');
}
$(allImages[index]).addClass(SELECTED);
var allButtons = $widget.find('.buttonStyle');
allButtons.removeClass('selected');
$(allButtons[index]).addClass('selected');
taRecord.trk("shopping_carousel_select", false, allImages[index]);
}

trackAction = "shopping_carousel_click";
}
taRecord.setEvtCookieAndPath(trackAction);
}

selectImage: _selectImage,
advanceImage: _advanceImage,
trackCarouselClick: _trackCarouselClick
};

define('utils/ellipsis', ["lib/jquery-amd"], function($) {
'use strict';
var _makeEllipsis = function(element, callback) {
if (element == null) {
return;
}
var ELLIPSIS = "\u2026";
var $target = $(element);
var divh = $target.height();
var originalText = $target.data('overview');
var start = 0;
var end = originalText.length;
var lastLenAtHeight = end;
$target.text(originalText);
if (element.scrollHeight > divh) {
while (end - start > 1) {
var mid = Math.floor((start + end) / 2);
var temp = originalText.substr(0, mid) + ELLIPSIS;
$target.text(temp);
if (element.scrollHeight <= divh) {
start = mid;
lastLenAtHeight = mid;
}
else {
end = mid;
}
}
$target.text(originalText.substr(0, lastLenAtHeight) + ELLIPSIS);
}
if (callback) {
callback(originalText.length - lastLenAtHeight);
}
};
var initEllipsis = function(element, callback) {
_makeEllipsis(element, callback);
$( window ).resize(function() {
_makeEllipsis(element, callback);
});
};
return {
initEllipsis: initEllipsis
};

define('shelves/shelfEventHandlers', ["lib/jquery-amd", "ta", "ta/util/Element", "utils/urlDecoder"],
function($, ta, taElement, urlDecode) {
'use strict';
var shelvesInView = [];
function _handleShelfTracking(element) {
var trackingPageProperty = element.getAttribute('data-tpp');
var trackingPageAction = element.getAttribute('data-tpact') || "shelf_in_view";
var trackingProductAttribute = element.getAttribute('data-tpatt');
var trackingProductId = element.getAttribute('data-tpid');
ta.trackEventOnPage(trackingPageProperty, trackingPageAction, trackingProductAttribute, trackingProductId);
}
function _handleScrollEvent() {
var shelfContainers = $(".shelf_title");
if (!shelfContainers) {
return;
}
shelfContainers.each(function (index) {
var shelf = shelfContainers[index];
if (shelvesInView.indexOf(shelf) === -1 && taElement.isScrolledIntoView(shelf)) {
_handleShelfTracking(shelf);
shelvesInView.push(shelf);
}
});
}
function _initImpressionTracking() {
_handleScrollEvent();
}
function _openUrl(element, sameTab) {
if (sameTab) {
window.location = urlDecode.getUrl(element);
} else {
window.open(urlDecode.getUrl(element), '_blank');
}
}
function _initListeners(name, initCall) {
if (!ta.SHELF_EVENT_INITIALIZED) {
ta.SHELF_EVENT_INITIALIZED = {};
}
if (!ta.SHELF_EVENT_INITIALIZED[name]) {
initCall();
ta.SHELF_EVENT_INITIALIZED[name] = true;
}
}
function _initDefaultShelfListeners() {
_initScrollEvent();
_initSeeAllTracking();
_initSeeAllEventHandlers();
_initSeeAnItemTracking();
_initSeeAnItemEventHandlers();
}
function _initScrollEvent() {
_initListeners('scrollEvent', function() {
_initImpressionTracking();
window.addEventListener("scroll", _handleScrollEvent);
});
}
function _initSeeAllTracking() {
_initListeners('seeAllTracking', function() {
ta.on('track_shelf_see_all_click_event', function(event, element) {
_handleShelfTracking(element);
});
});
}
function _initSeeAnItemTracking() {
_initListeners('seeAllItemTracking', function() {
ta.on('track_shelf_item_click_event', function(event, element) {
_handleShelfTracking(element);
});
});
}
function _initSeeAllEventHandlers(eventCallBack) {
_initListeners('seeAllEventHandlers', function() {
ta.on('shelf_see_all_click_event', function(event, element, sameTab, noTracking) {
new Event(event).preventDefault();
if (!noTracking) {
_handleShelfTracking(element);
}
if (eventCallBack) {
eventCallBack(event, element);
} else {
_openUrl(element, sameTab);
}
})
});
}
function _initSeeAnItemEventHandlers(eventCallBack) {
_initListeners('seeAnItemEventHandlers', function() {
ta.on('shelf_item_click_event', function(event, element, sameTab, noTracking) {
new Event(event).preventDefault();
if (!noTracking) {
_handleShelfTracking(element);
}
if (eventCallBack) {
eventCallBack(event, element);
} else {
_openUrl(element, sameTab);
}
});
});
}
return {
initShelfListeners: _initDefaultShelfListeners,
initSeeAllTracking: _initSeeAllTracking,
initSeeAnItemTracking: _initSeeAnItemTracking,
initSeeAllEventHandlers: _initSeeAllEventHandlers,
initSeeAnItemEventHandlers: _initSeeAnItemEventHandlers,
initScrollEvent: _initScrollEvent
};
});
define('utils/geolocation', ['vanillajs'], function() {
'use strict';
var canRequestLocation = function() {
return typeof navigator != 'undefined' && typeof navigator.geolocation != 'undefined';
};
var requestLocation = function(onSuccess, onFailure) {
if (typeof onSuccess !== "function") {
return;
}
if (canRequestLocation()) {
navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
function(response) {
onSuccess({
latitude: response.coords.latitude,
longitude: response.coords.longitude
});
},
function(error) {
if (typeof onFailure === "function") {
onFailure(error);
}
});
} else {
onFailure(new Error("Location services not available"));
}
};
return {
canRequestLocation: canRequestLocation,
requestLocation: requestLocation
};
});require(['ta/p13n/placements'], function(placements) {
var define = placements.define.bind(placements,'mobile_attraction_coverpage','handlers',['handlers']);
/**
* Events:
* event.placement.mobileAttractionCoverage.inDestination - reload contents with geolocation.
*/
define([
'placement',
'lib/jquery-amd',
'ta',
'shelves/shelfEventHandlers',
'utils/geolocation',
'common/trackingStreams',
'ta/Core/TA.Event',
'ta/util/ajaxPreserves',
'ta/prwidgets']
, function(
placement,
$,
ta,
shelfEventHandlers,
GeoLocation,
Tracking,
taEvent,
ajaxPreserves,
prwidgets) {
"use strict";
ta.queueForReady(function() {
shelfEventHandlers.initShelfListeners();
taEvent.on('event.placement.mobileAttractionCoverage.inDestination', inDestination);
taEvent.on('update-' + placement.id, _updateCoverPages);
});
function _updateCoverPages(content) {
var parentContainer = document.getElementById(placement.id);
var contentElement = parentContainer.querySelector('.update-wrapper');
ajaxPreserves.setContentElement(contentElement, content, true);
prwidgets.initWidgets(placement.id);
}
function _isResponseEmpty(htmlText) {
return ! /<div class="coverpage">/.test(htmlText);
}
function _requestAjaxPlacementSuccess(responseText) {
_stopLoading();
if (_isResponseEmpty(responseText)) {
Tracking.trackEvent(placement.name, 'request', 'nocontent', placement.location_id);
return;
}
Tracking.trackEvent(placement.name, 'request', 'success', placement.location_id);
var container = document.getElementById(placement.id);
if (container) {
// setting innerHTML is required in order for handlers to setup properly.
container.innerHTML = responseText;
}
if (prwidgets) {
prwidgets.initWidgets(placement.id);
}
}
function _requestAjaxPlacementFailure(error) {
_stopLoading();
Tracking.trackEvent(placement.name, 'request', 'failed', placement.location_id);
}
function _stopLoading() {
$('#' + placement.id + ' .ui_spinner.large').addClass('hidden');
}
function _startLoading() {
$('#' + placement.id + ' .ui_spinner.large').removeClass('hidden');
}
function inDestination() {
if (GeoLocation.canRequestLocation())
{
_startLoading();
GeoLocation.requestLocation(function(geopoint) {
var params = {};
Tracking.trackEvent(placement.name, 'geolocation', 'success', placement.location_id);
$.extend(params, geopoint);
placement.requestAJAXPlacement(_requestAjaxPlacementSuccess, _requestAjaxPlacementFailure, params);
},
function(error) {
_stopLoading();
Tracking.trackEvent(placement.name, 'geolocation', 'failed', placement.location_id);
});
}
}
return {
inDestination: inDestination
};

define('ta/util/RecordInterruption', ['vanillajs', 'ta/Core/TA.Record', 'ta/util/Error'], function(vanilla, track, error) {
'use strict';
var GA_REC_MODULE = 'interruption_record';
var VALID_TYPES = [
'popup',
'popunder',
'gate',
'other'
];
var _err = function(msg, eobj) {
error.record(eobj, msg, null, null);
};
var _isValidType = function(type) {
for (var i = 0; i < VALID_TYPES.length; i++) {
if (type === VALID_TYPES[i]) {
return true;
}
}
return false;
};
return {
record: function(type, name) {
try {
if (!_isValidType(type)) {
_err("ta/util/RecordInterruption: Invalid type");
} else if (!name) {
_err("ta/util/RecordInterruption: Name cannot be null or blank");
} else {
track.trackEventOnPage(GA_REC_MODULE, type, name.replace(',', ''), 0, true);
}
} catch (e) {
_err("ta/util/RecordInterruption: exception tracking event", e);
}
}
};
});
require(['ta/p13n/placements'], function(placements) {
var define = placements.define.bind(placements,'qualtrics_survey','handlers',['handlers']);
/** Private javascript for qualtrics survey placement
* We want to show on the 2nd pageview, no more than once every 30 days
* The div id is generated from the qualtrics site-intercept code.
* The placement render will decide which survey to displace.
*/
define([
"placement",
"lib/jquery-amd",
"ta",
'ta/Core/TA.LocalStorage',
'page-model',
'ta/util/RecordInterruption',
'ta/support/Qualtrics',
'utils/throttle'
],
function (placement, $, ta, taLocalStore, model, recordInterruption, taQualtrics, throttle) {
"use strict";
ta.queueForLoad(function () {
// For surveys that should hide when the user begins to scroll, this is the how much give they have
var SCROLL_BUFFER = 318;
// Campaign ID for event tracking
var CAMPAIGN_ID = 'qualtrics_surveys';
taQualtrics.setSmartSurvey(!!placement.params.smartSurvey);
taQualtrics.updatePageViews();
if (taLocalStore.enabled && ( taQualtrics.isDebug() || taQualtrics.canDisplaySmart() || ( !taQualtrics.getSmartSurvey() && taQualtrics.canDisplay() ) )) {
var surveyKey = placement.params.surveyId;
var surveyContainerClassName = '.' + surveyKey + '_InfoBarContainer';
var surveyName = placement.params.surveyName;
var surveyProperties = 'Qualtrics_Survey' + '|' + window.pageServlet + '|' + surveyName;
if (placement.params.smartSurvey) {
var getSurveyProperties = function (_ss, _qa) {
return _ss + '|' + ['sc-' + _qa.getSessionCount(), 'ir-' + _qa.getInterceptReqs(), 'iv-' + _qa.getInterceptViews(), 'pv-'+_qa.getPageViews()].join('|');
};
$('body').on('qxInterceptShown', function () {
ta.trackEventOnPage(CAMPAIGN_ID, 'interceptShown', getSurveyProperties(surveyProperties, taQualtrics), null, true);
taQualtrics.updateInterceptViews();
taQualtrics.updateSessionCount();
});
$('body').on('qxInterceptAccept', function () {
ta.trackEventOnPage(CAMPAIGN_ID, 'interceptAccept', getSurveyProperties(surveyProperties, taQualtrics), null, false);
taQualtrics.setResponded(true);
});
$('body').on('qxInterceptDecline', function () {
ta.trackEventOnPage(CAMPAIGN_ID, 'interceptDecline', getSurveyProperties(surveyProperties, taQualtrics), null, false);
taQualtrics.setResponded(true);
});
}
if (surveyKey) {
taQualtrics.displaySurvey(surveyKey);
recordInterruption.record('popup', surveyProperties, taQualtrics.getPageViews());
if (placement.params.smartSurvey) {
taQualtrics.updateInterceptReqs();
}
// TV-1243 - Mobile Surveys cover a commerce component, so they should be hidden when the user begins to scroll
if (placement.params.hideOnScroll) {
var hide = function () {
var scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop || document.body.scrollTop;
if (scrollTop > SCROLL_BUFFER) {
$(surveyContainerClassName).hide();
}
};
$(window).on('scroll', throttle(hide, 100));
}
}
}
});
return {
};
});

taRecord.trackEventOnPage('TopNav', 'mytrips_dropdown_cancel');
if (elmt) {
$(elmt).find('.ui_icon').removeClass('hovering');
}
});
placementEl.find('.trips-flyout-container').removeClass('hide-arrow');
}, 0);
});
});
}.bind(placementEl);
// Profile Link: When clicking on a utility link, open the submenu, if one is available
placementEl.on('click', '.global-nav-utility-activator', function(evt) {
var elm = $(this);
// Is there a submenu to show?
var menuEl = placementEl.find(elm.data('element')).clone();
if (!menuEl.length) {
return;
}
if (oldOverlay) {
if (oldOverlay.sourceElement == this){
oldOverlay.isOpen() ? oldOverlay.hide('close') : oldOverlay.show();
return; // don't re-open the same overlay.
}
else {
oldOverlay.hide('new-overlay');
}
}
// Create a new overlay
menuEl = menuEl.clone();
var reqs = ['trjs!overlays/Overlay',
'trjs!overlays/styles/flyout',
'trjs!overlays/options/closeOnDocClick',
'trjs!overlays/position',
'trjs!overlays/options/autoReposition'
];
require(reqs, function(Overlay, Flyout, CloseOnDocClick, Position, AutoReposition) {
var overlay = new Overlay(elm[0], new Flyout(menuEl[0], 'global-nav-flyout global-nav-utility'), CloseOnDocClick, elm.data('nav-2018-enabled') ? Position.bottomLeft([(elm.width()/2)-34, 8]) : Position.bottomLeft([-20, -3]), AutoReposition);
overlay.domParent = placementEl.find('.global-nav-overlays-container')[0];
overlay.show();
elm.addClass('menu-open');
$(evt.currentTarget).find('.ui_icon').addClass('hovering');
overlay.on('hide', function() {
elm.removeClass('menu-open');
$(evt.currentTarget).find('.ui_icon').removeClass('hovering');
});
oldOverlay = overlay;
});
});

// Mobile Web Global Nav Persistent Icons
function checkForPersistentIcons() {
var offsetPosition = $(window).scrollTop();
if (navIcons.length) {
// A - Sideways default state: Logo and icons together, geo pill on second line
// B - Sideways 1st scroll (down): Icons animate to geo pill, logo scrolls out of view
// C - Sideways 2nd scroll (down): Icons locked to geo pill, all elements scroll out of view
//
// A - Internal default state: No logo, geo pill and icons on first line
// B - Internal 1st scroll (down): Icons locked to geo pill, all elements scroll out of view
// C - Internal 1st scroll (up): Icons animate to logo, logo scrolls into view
//
// Adjust icons to placements: Logo then Geopill when available
if (pill.is(':visible')) {
var calculatePlacementInView = placementEl.height() - offsetPosition;
// Keep icons confined to scrollable area on DW & MW (avoids snap-into-view on MW)
if (offsetPosition <= 0) {
navIcons.css({
'position': 'absolute',
'top': 0
});
}
// As long as the icons are w/n the scrollable area, animate position of icons
if (calculatePlacementInView > 0) {
if (offsetPosition > 0 && offsetPosition <= 50) {
navIcons.css({
'position': 'absolute',
'top': offsetPosition,
'bottom': 'auto'
});
}
// When the icons reach the end of the scrollable area, lock them to the geo pill
else if (calculatePlacementInView <= 50) {
navIcons.css({
'position': 'absolute',
'top': 'auto',
'bottom': 0
});
}
}
}
}
}
// Auto scroll to desired position based on traffic type
function positionSecondView() {
var hideLogo = $('.second-view', placementEl);
var offsetPosition = $(window).scrollTop();
if (navIcons.length) {
logo.css({
'display': 'block'
});
if (hideLogo.length && pill.is(':visible')) {
offsetPosition = persistentIcons.height() - logo.height();
window.scroll(0, offsetPosition);
navIcons.css({
'position': 'absolute',
'top': 'auto',
'bottom': 0
});
}
}
}
// Global Nav Persistent Single-line Header
function checkForPersistentGlobalNav() {
var persistentGlobalNav = $('.global-nav-persistent', placementEl);
if (persistentGlobalNav.length) {
persistentGlobalNav.toggleClass('fixed', $(window).scrollTop() > placementEl.offset().top);
}
if ($trip_search_geopill_slave[0] && !$trip_search_geopill_slave[0].dataset.masterGeopill) {
radioScrollGeoPill.on('hide-on-header', function(shouldHide) {
$trip_search_geopill_slave.parent().toggleClass('hidden', shouldHide);
});
// TODO Fix in NAV-6886
/* The following commented out block is from quick links on header scroll state logic */
// var $candy_bar_links_el = $('#QUICK_LINKS');
// var $global_nav_bottom_header = placementEl.find('.global-nav-bottom');
//
// if ($candy_bar_links_el.length && $global_nav_bottom_header.length) {
//   $global_nav_bottom_header.toggleClass('hidden', $(window).scrollTop() < $candy_bar_links_el.offset().top + 20);
// }
}
}
// Default scroll position for responsive views
positionSecondView();
var positionGlobalNav = throttle(checkForPersistentGlobalNav, 100);
$(window).scroll( function() {
checkForPersistentIcons();
positionGlobalNav();
});
// Tracking for links in submenus works by looking up the active-menu-trigger
// (link that triggered the dropdown) and using it's tracking-label as a prefix
placementEl.on('click', 'a.global-nav-link[data-tracking-label]', function(event) {
var trackingLabel = $(event.target).data('trackingLabel');
// Handle links to /# (Help Center) or links opening new window
require(['trjs!ta/Core/TA.Record'], function(taRecord) {
if("HelpDesk" === trackingLabel || event.target.target == '_blank') {
taRecord.trackEventOnPage(TRACKING_CATEGORY, 'click', trackingLabel);
} else {
taRecord.setEvtCookie(TRACKING_CATEGORY, 'click', trackingLabel, 0, event.target.href);
}
});
});
return {
checkForPersistentIcons: checkForPersistentIcons,
checkForPersistentGlobalNav: checkForPersistentGlobalNav
};
});
});
define('trcore', ['vanillajs', 'ns-exporter', 'ta/util/Cookie'],
function(vanilla, nsExporter, taCookie) {
var globalFuncs = {};
function _addEvent(name, fn) {
if (window.addEventListener) {
window.addEventListener(name, fn);
}
else if (window.attachEvent) {
window.attachEvent('on'+name, fn);
}
}
globalFuncs.registerOnLoad = function(fn, name) {
if (require.defined('ta/Core/TA.Event')) {
require('ta/Core/TA.Event').queueForLoad(fn, name);
}
else {
_addEvent('load', fn);
}
};
globalFuncs.registerOnUnload = function(fn) {
_addEvent('unload', fn);
};
globalFuncs.getScrollOffset = function() {
return [
window.pageXOffset || document.documentElement.scrollLeft,
window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop
];
};
globalFuncs.setOneTimeCookie = function(key,value) {
taCookie.write(key, value, 5000, null, cookieDomain);
return true;
};
globalFuncs.setOneTimeCookieOnFQDN = function(key,value) {
taCookie.write(key, value, 5000);
return true;
};
nsExporter.exportTo(globalFuncs, window||global);
return globalFuncs;
});

define(['placement', 'vanillajs', 'trcore', 'ta/Core/TA.Record', 'utils/browserutils', 'utils/throttle'],
function(placement, vanilla, trCore, taRecord, browserUtils, throttle) {

, FALLBACK_URL = browserUtils.Platform.ios ? 'https://lnk0.com/wNtsAl' : 'https://lnk0.com/sYxFZ9'
, PLACEMENT_ELMT = document.querySelector('#' + placement.id)
, PLACEMENT_CLASSNAME = PLACEMENT_ELMT.className
, UNIVERSAL_LINK_BASE_URL = "https://api.tripadvisor.cn"

}

_showSmartButton();

search = (!!search ? search + '&' : '?') + 'm=' + MCID;

}

trCore.setOneTimeCookie('OpenAppFailure', encodeURIComponent(FALLBACK_URL));
}
// Use a short timeout to allow tracking code to execute
setTimeout(function() {
window.location.href = !!APP_LINK_URL ? APP_LINK_URL : _buildUniversalLinkWithMcid();
}, 200);
}
, _init = function() {
setTimeout(_showSmartButton, 100);
PLACEMENT_ELMT.addEventListener('click', _handleButtonClicked, false);
window.addEventListener('scroll', throttle(_handleScroll, 100), false);
}
;
trCore.registerOnLoad(_init, 'OpenAppSmartButton');

define("cpm/AdBlockDetect", ["lib/jquery-amd","utils/browserutils","ta/Core/TA.Event","ta/Core/TA.Record","ta/util/Error"],
function( $, Browser, taEvent, taRecord, taError) {
'use strict';
var exports = {};
var _testImg;
var _isPixelLoadError;
var _logged = false;
var _cdn = window.CDNHOST || "";
var _pixelUrl = "/img2/x.gif?&ads=1&adsize=2&adslot=3&rnd=";
var _generatePixel = function() {
var rnd = Math.floor(Math.random() * 100000);
return $('<img src="' + _cdn + _pixelUrl + rnd + '" style="position:absolute" class="ad ad_column" height="0" width="0" />');
};
var _getAdCount = function() {
var count = document.querySelectorAll(".gptAd:not(.inactive)").length;
if (screen.width < 768) {
count += document.querySelectorAll(".inline_ad_wrapper").length;
}
return count;
};
var _log = function(blocked, trackingLabel, trackUnblocked){
if (!_logged && trackingLabel){
if (blocked || trackUnblocked) {
taRecord.trackEventOnPage(trackingLabel, Browser.name, blocked, _getAdCount(), false);
}
_logged = true;
}
};
var _detect = function(onDetectedHandler, trackingLabel, trackUnblocked, isLoadError){
if (typeof isLoadError != undefined) {
_isPixelLoadError = isLoadError;
}
if (_testImg){
var blocked = _isPixelLoadError ? true : !_testImg[0].offsetParent;
_log(blocked, trackingLabel, trackUnblocked);
if (blocked) {
onDetectedHandler();
}
}
};
exports.runIfDetected = function(onDetectedHandler, trackingLabel, trackUnblocked) {
if ( typeof onDetectedHandler != "function") {
taError.record(null, "runIfDetected requires a function");
return;
}
taEvent.queueForLoad( function() {
_logged = false;
if (_testImg) {
_detect(onDetectedHandler, trackingLabel, trackUnblocked);
} else {
_testImg = _generatePixel();
_testImg.on("load", function(){ _detect(onDetectedHandler, trackingLabel, trackUnblocked, false); });
_testImg.on("error", function(){ _detect(onDetectedHandler, trackingLabel, trackUnblocked, true); });
$("body").append(_testImg);
}
}, "AdBlockDetect");
};
return exports;
});

define('ta/util/ActionRecord', ['vanillajs', 'ta/util/Deferred', 'utils/ajax', 'ns-exporter', 'ta/Core/TA.Record'],
function(vanilla, Deferred, ajax, nsExporter, taRecord) {
var exports = {
record: function record(action, options, track){
return _record('/ActionRecord', action, options, track);
},
recordPlus: function recordPlus(action, options, track){
return _record('/ActionRecordPlus', action, options, track);
},
recordPid: function recordPid(pid) {
new ajax('/ActionRecord?pid=' + pid);
}
};
function _record(url, action, options, track) {
var deferred = new Deferred();
if (!options) {
options = {};
}
var ops = {
url: options.url || url,
method: options.method || 'get',
data: {
action: action
},
success: function(response) {
options.onSuccess && options.onSuccess(response);
deferred.resolve(response);
},
error: function(response) {
options.onFailure && options.onFailure(response);
deferred.reject(response);
}
};
for (var k in options) {
if (options.hasOwnProperty(k) && !ops.hasOwnProperty(k)) {
ops[k] = options[k];
}
else if (k == 'data') {
for (k in options.data) {
if (options.data.hasOwnProperty(k)) {
ops.data[k] = options.data[k];
}
}
}
}
if (track) {
var params = taRecord._toEvtParams(track);
for (k in params) {
if (params.hasOwnProperty(k)) {
ops.data[k] = params[k];
}
}
}
ajax(ops);
if (track) {
taRecord._trackEventAfterAjax(track);
}
return deferred.promise();
}
nsExporter.exportTo(exports, "ta.util.action");
return exports;
});

return;

Track.record(actionPrefix + action)
.always(function() {
window.location = link.attr("href");
});
} else {
Track.record(actionPrefix + action);
}
});
